of  Qinghai,  served  as  a  ﬁnancial 
force  supporting 
development  of  Qinghai  Province  and  serving  small  and 
medium and micro-sized enterprises and rural and urban 
residents.  In  the  past  20  years,  we  have  been  deepen
the reform and innovation, achieved transformation from 
urban  collective  ﬁnancial  organization  to  modernized 
stock  commercial  system,  ﬁnished  3  rounds  of  increase 
in  capital  and  share,  improved  the  modern  corporate 
governing system, covered business network from Xining 
to  the  whole  province,  enabled  main  electronic  network 
service  channels  and  developed  the  products  from 
deposit and loan at the beginning to linking of loan, debt 
and  investment  online  and  ofﬂine.  The  inclusive  ﬁnance 
and  green  ﬁnance  in  conformity  with  actual  situations 
of  Qinghai  Province  and  with  features  of  the  Bank  of
Qinghai  achieved  great  development,  leap  forward  and 
it has improved comprehensive capability. In the past 20 
years, we have been concerning the local situations andthe  civilians,  exercising  corporate  social  responsibilities
with  senses  of  politics  and  mission,  actively  devoted 
to  getting  rid  of  poverty  and  helping  those  who  need
help,  paying  tax  of  2.507  billion  Yuan  in  total  and
denoting  more  than  20  million  Yuan  to  society.  At  the
20th  Anniversary,  we  follow  the  principle  of  running
the  anniversary  ceremony  with  frugalness,  concern  the
civilians  in  Tibetan  areas,  denoted  3.884  million  Yuan
to  medical  industry  in  Yushu  and  education  in  Guoluo,
and  demonstrated  local  bank’s  undertaking  and  the
feeling  of  serving  the  people.  In  the  past  20  years,  we
have been following the principle of Party building guide
and harmonic development, the leader core and political
core of the Party Committee of the Bank play key roles.
The  corporate  culture  building  is  deeply  rooted  in  mind,
all  the  staff  share  the  corporate  culture  development
achievements, and the senses of gaining, happiness and 
belonging have been enhanced and the Bank of Qinghai
is the homeland of more than 1700 staff of the Bank.The  20  years’  development  of  the  Bank  of  Qinghai 
is  overall  and  innovative,  and  the  transformation  is
profound  and  fundamental.  At  present,  the  Bank  of
Qinghai  stands  at  a  new  historical  starting  point,  faces
new  era,  new  journey  and  new  challenges  and  the 
Bank  of  Qinghai  will  contribute  more.  We  will  stay  true 
to  the  mission  and  remember  our  mission,  centering 
the  three  tasks  of  serving  entity  economy,  preventing
and  controlling  ﬁnancial  risks  and  deepening  ﬁnancial
reform  proposed  by  the  central  government,  reform

comprehensive  ﬁnancial  service  capabilities  to  satisfy
customers’  ﬁnancial  requirements  and  contribute  more

2.18%III. Abstract of Main Financial Data8.  Non-conforming loan and adopted measures at the end of the periodAt  the  end  of  the  reporting  period,  total  loan  of  the  Company  was  46.9960061  billion  Yuan.  According  to  the
5-level  classiﬁcation  calibers,  46.0785187  billion  Yuan  was  classiﬁed  as  normal  and  concern  types,  accounting  for
98.05% of total amount; amount of the last 3 types was 917.4874 million Yuan, accounting for 1.95% and the non-
conforming loan rate was increased by 0.11%.In  year  2017,  facing  “double  increasing  of  non-conforming  loan”,  in  particular  to  the  severe  conditions  of
continuous  non-conforming,  the  Company  adhered  to  the  principle  of  managing  existing  and  increment  loans  and 
adopted  measures  to  compress  and  control  scale  of  non-conforming  loan.  Firstly,  the  Company  implemented  the
national  macroscopic  regulating  policy,  optimized  the  credit  loan  trends,  improved  technology  transformation, 
upgrading  and  science&  technology  innovation  for  strategic  emerging  industries  and  traditional  industrial  technology 
renovation,  accelerated  quitting  of  loan  for  restricted  industries  and  strictly  controlled  application  of  the  loan;

2017年，中国人民银行继续实施稳健中性的货币政策，密切关注流动性形势和市场预期变化，加强预调微
调和与市场沟通，为稳增长、调结构、促改革、惠民生、去杠杆、抑泡沫、防风险营造了适宜的货币金融环境。
综合运用逆回购、中期借贷便利等工具，维护银行体系流动性基本稳定。宣布对普惠金融实施定向降准政策，运
用支农支小再贷款、扶贫再贷款和抵押补充贷款等工具并发挥信贷政策的结构引导作用，支持经济结构调整和
转型升级，将更多金融资源配置到经济社会发展的重点领域和薄弱环节。3、  业 务 发 展 综 述公 司 业 务 　2017 年，本 公 司 不 断 优 化 金 融 服 务
能力和水平，加大资金投放，全面推动公司业务稳步
发展。截至2017年末，全行对公存款余额达4,201,872
万 元，较 年 初 新 增 228,110万 元，全 行 对 公 贷 款 余 额
4,304,050万元，较年初新增574,835万元。投行业务作
为公司业务转型期的重点业务，全年实际新增投放达
365,000万 元，其 中 产 业 基 金 业 务 新 增 投 放315,000万
元，私 募 债 新 增 投 放50,000万 元，截 至2017年 末 投 资
总规模已达1,329,500万元，投资余额达849,000万元，
对利润新增起到了重要的支持作用，更为本公司密切
银政企合作关系、相互促进、共同发展提供了新的方
式及方法。“票据综合处理平台”系统成功上线以及本
公司“电子商业汇票系统”与上海票交所系统移交切换
的顺利完成，也对完善公司业务服务体系，健全公司
业务品种起到了十分重要的作用，更为本公司竭力支
持全省产业转型升级和经济社会发展提供了源源不断

卡贫困户发放了“530”扶贫小额贷款408万元，加快了当地贫困户脱贫致富的进程。上线微信银行小微及消费贷
款网上预申请功能，大力推广“银税贷”“商圈贷”“联合贷”等特色小微贷款业务。截至2017年末，个人存款余额
2,147,212万元，较年初新增297,329万元，增长16.07%，个人存款市场份额继续稳步提升。小微及个人贷款余额
1,304,825.9万元，其中小微及“FS农贷”贷款余额1,097,874.56万元，较年初新增165,361.02万元 ；个人消费类贷
款余额206,951.34万元，较年初新增40,992万元，全行信用卡总量达到58,426张。资金业务　2017年，本公司积极适应经济新常态，着力支持实体经济发展，运用同业平台和金融工具，形成
线上线下结合，交易多元化、市场化程度高的同业业务体系，切实提高了流动性管理水平和资金效益。持续发挥
同业渠道和品牌优势，兼顾流动性、安全性和收益性的平衡，保持资产负债有效增长。加快推进绿色金融债发行
工作，进一步拓展市场化融资途径。全年累计办理金融市场业务1.08万笔、金额65,782,415万元，金融市场业务
创利能力不断提升，全行资产负债规模、期限、品种的调剂作用持续强化。加大理财产品创新力度，推动综合理
财平台开放式产品模块顺利上线，推出本公司首支7天开放式理财产品，丰富了理财产品体系。截至2017年末，

(cid:16843)(cid:11901)(cid:13262)(cid:11741)(cid:12468)(cid:11712)(cid:16264)(cid:7236)At the end of May and beginning of June, 2017, according to district demarcation and its actual situations,
the  Bank  of  Qinghai  combined  Chengxi  Sub-branch  and  Guchengtai  Sub-branch,  renamed  Shengli  Sub-branch 
into  Chengbei  Sub-branch,  shaped  ﬁve  administrative  banks  such  as  Chengzhong,  Chengxi,  Chengdong,
Chengbei  and  Haihu  New  District.  The  layout  in  Xining  is  more  reasonable  and  operation  and  management  are 
more efﬁcient.ANNUAL REPORT 201719IV. The Management’s discussion and analysis1.  Scope of businessThe  scope  of  business  of  the  Company  includes:  public  deposit  taking;  issuing  short-term,  medium-term
and  long-term  loan;  handling  domestic  settlement;  handling  notes  discounting;  issuing  ﬁnancial  bonds;  agency  of
discounting and sales of government bonds; engaging in inter-bank borrowing; providing payment and collection and 
insurance agency; providing safe business; handling consigned deposit business for fund used for circulation of fund
for  local  revenue  credit;  bank  card  business;  sales  and  purchasing  and  consigned  sales  and  purchasing  of  foreign
currency; settlement of exchange, exchange surrendering and national treasury agency business; fund sales business;
other business approved by the banking industry supervision organization of the State Council.2.  Changes of external business environment and the inﬂuences during the reporting period2.1 Macroscopic economic situations

development into high-quality development and economic development quality was improved continuously.2.2 Changes of supervision environment
In  year  2017,  ﬁnancial  supervision  was  called  the  “most  strict”  supervision  year  in  history.  The  State  Council
established  the  Financial  Stability  and  Development  Commission,  which  issued  ﬁnancial  supervision  policy  on  asset
management  industry,  bank,  public  placement  and  insurance  and  issued  large-amount  tickets,  which  marked  that,
the  ﬁnancial  cycle  was  reverted  and  entered  a  new  era  of  deﬂation.  The  asset  management  business  was  changed
fundamentally and was transformed into the mode of “being consigned by others to ﬁnance for them”. Risk favorites of 
organizational transaction were transformed from radical to conservative, and ﬁnance away from virtual to physical was 
accelerated. Financial institutions entered substantial reduced balance sheet, resulting in more importance of liquidity
risks and liabilities management, and the overtaking era for medium and small-sized bank ended.2.3 Change of monetary policy 
In year 2017, the People’s Bank of China continued to carry out the stable and neutral monetary policy, closely
focused on liquidity situations and market expectation changes, emphasized on pre-adjustment and micro-adjustment,
communicated with market and created a proper monetary and ﬁnancial environment for stabilizing growth, regulating
structure, promoting reform, beneﬁting the livelihood, de-leverage and preventing risks. Use of reverse repurchasing,
medium-term  loan  convenience  and  other  tools  is  deployed  to  maintain  stability  of  liquidity  of  the  bank  system. 
Targeted  deposit  reserve  ratio  was  reduced  for  inclusive  ﬁnance,  the  re-loan  for  supporting  agriculture,  small-sized
enterprises, poverty relief re-loan and supplementary mortgage loan shall be used to play the structural leading role of 
the  credit  loan  policy  to  support  economic  restructuring  and  economic  transformation,  and  more  ﬁnancial  resources
were conﬁgured to key ﬁelds and vulnerable processes for economic and social development.3.  Summary of business developmentCorporate  business In  year  2017,  the  Company  optimized  ﬁnancial  service  capabilities  and  proﬁciencies,

operation risk, information science& technology risk and reputation risk. In year 2017, based on “deeply implementing
deployments  and  requirements  by  the  central,  provincial  Party  Committees,  Governments  and  the  Party  Committee
of  the  Bank,  centering  improving  quality  and  increasing  efﬁciency,  deeply  implementing  the  Guide  to  Overall  Risk 
Management,  deepening  reform  and  innovation,  providing  precise  target  support,  improving  risk  management  and 
control,  intensifying  comprehensive  service  guarantee,  advancing  featuring,  exquisite  and  differentiation  building 
and  creating  new  situations  for  stable  development  of  the  Company”  and  the  requirements  “focusing  more  on 
risk  prevention  and  control  than  ever”,  the  Company  highlighted  the  prudence  management  philosophy,  improved 
mechanism,  implemented  measures  comprehensively,  improved  risk  prevention,  control  and  dissolving  capabilities,
stayed at the bottom line of preventing systematic ﬁnancial risks and realized safe and healthy operation.4.1 Credit risks 
In  year  2017,  to  intensify  the  credit  loan  risk  management  and  improve  lean  risk  management,  the  Company
continued to increase management and control over credit loan. The Credit Risk Commission of the Company exercised 
duties  effectively,  convoked  16  meetings  in  the  year,  timely  reviewed  potential  risky  loan  handling  solutions,  ﬁnancing
guarantee  company  access,  renewal  and  other  key  issues.  The  “three-inspection”  system  was  strictly  executed  for
the  loan,  the  key  account  risk  monitoring  meeting  was  convoked  in  each  quarter,  the  business  risk  was  continuously
concerned, management requirements were proposed to the branches through written supervision and notiﬁcation, risk 
points  and  insufﬁciency  to  be  concerned  should  be  prompted,  implementation  by  the  branches  should  be  supervised
and 63 periodicals of key account risk supervision and announcement were issued. The national and local supply-side
reform  policies  and  measures  were  implemented  to  support  the  in-province  industrial  enterprises  to  stabilize  growth, 
adjust structure, increase beneﬁts, actively support high-quality enterprises, and loan withdrawal, reduction and proper 
scale were applied to industrial enterprises with difﬁculties in a short term but products still competitive, and the zombie
enterprises; small and micro-enterprises were actively supported, the support policy was implemented to support normal
fund requirements of small and micro-enterprises, and the loan was timely renewed to dissolve the business risks from
being  short  of  fund.  As  for  industrial  enterprises,  small  and  micro-enterprises  difﬁcult  in  repaying  the  loan,  different
policies were applied, many meetings on dissolving risks and supervision were carried out, and the leaders of the Bank 
took  charge  of  supervision  for  more  than  10  years,  as  well  as  64  times  of  departmental  supervision  to  achieve  the
expected results. Of them, existing loan which was overdue for more than 90 days 85.663 million Yuan in year 2016 was
recovered and loan of 91 million Yuan overdue for more than 90 million Yuan in year 2017 was rolled back. The credit
extension assets and risk were classiﬁed to reﬂect quality of credit loan assets of the Bank.4.2 Liquidity risks 
In  year  2017,  on  the  preconditions  of  risk  control,  the  Company  guided  and  controlled  total  volume,  structure, 
cost  and  proceed  of  assets  and  liabilities  for  business  objectives.  Through  reinforcing  low-cost  liabilities  stability,ANNUAL REPORT 201723IV. The ﬁrst is interest risk. In year 2017, facing market risk situations of narrowing net interest difference of interest-
bearing assets, the Company utilized the internal fund transfer and pricing system, combined analysis and judgment 
of  market  interest  rate  trend,  priced  differentiation  of  fund  in  view  of  costs  and  proceeds,  performed  centralized
management  for  interest  rate  risk  and  liquidity  risk  and  effectively  improved  interest  rate  risks.  The  second  is 
exchange  rate  risk.  According  to  the  inter-bank  market  and  international  foreign  currency  market  prices  changes  on
the  dame,  the  Company  updated  the  international  settlement  system  and  core  business  system  to  avoid  exchange
rate  risks.  At  the  end  of  the  year  2017,  the  Company’s  cumulative  foreign  exchange  open  position  rate  was  0.31%,
which was in conformity with the supervision requirements. Thirdly, to prevent market risks effectively, the Company
planned  to  establish  the  product  pricing  system  and  improved  the  product  pricing  system  to  satisfy  the  pricing
management requirements for deposit and loan products and customer differentiation. Through application of ﬂexible
product  pricing  code,  costs  were  measured  for  each  deal  to  ensure  that  transaction  of  each  price  covered  fund 
cost,  operation  cost,  risk  cost,  capital  cost  and  tax  cost  etc.  Meanwhile,  the  scope  of  marketing  was  determined 
through customer relationship and product systems, use of data analyzing technique and identiﬁcation of customers’ 
favorites and customers’ behaviors, and product innovation and demarcation of customers were realized. According
to  the  market  interest  ﬂuctuation  and  transmission  mechanism,  inﬂuences  of  sensitive  assets  and  liabilities  revenues
and  expenditures  and  net  market  values  were  analyzed  to  adjust  pries  of  the  ﬁnancing  products,  correct  incorrect 
resources allocation, and make the business under controllable risks with proper pricing and maximum proceeds.4.4 Operation risks

the  Board  of  Directors,  the  Board  of  Supervisors  and  the  operation  tier,  systematized  and  embodied  the  Party 
Committee’s  orienting  and  collaborating  the  parties’  political  core  and  leadership  core,  shaped  the  “ﬁve-in-one” 
modernization  company  governing  system  of  Party  Committee  in  placement,  standardized  Shareholders’  General
Assembly,  healthy  Board  of  Directors,  effective  Board  of  Supervisors  and  responsible  operation  tier,  and  the 
Company’s governing structure becomes standardized and improved.1.1 Improving the Company’s fundamental system of governing 
In the year 2017, the Board of Directors of the Company fully played a key role in corporate governing, according 
to  the  latest  supervision  requirements  and  modern  corporate  governing  requirements  and  established  and  improved
the  Company’s  fundamental  governing  system.  The  Company  revised  the Articles  of  Association  of  the  Bank  of 
Qinghai,  Management  on  Authorization  of  the  Bank  of  Qinghai  (Edition  2016)  and Rules  and  Regulations  on  Basic 
Authorization of the Bank of Qinghai (Edition 2016).1.2 About shareholders and shareholders’ assembly 
In year 2017, the shareholders of the Company exercised power according to laws, rules and regulations and the
Articles of Association of the Bank of Qinghai, and exercised obligations strictly. Meanwhile, the Company established
and  improved  an  effective  channel  and  mechanism  with  shareholders,  took  shareholders’  opinions  and  suggestions,
and  ensured  that  all  the  shareholders’  were  entitled  to  knowing  rights,  participating  rights  and  voting  rights  for  key
issues and exercised the lawful rights and interests of the shareholders.In  year  2017,  strictly  in  accordance  with  the  Articles  of  Association  of  the  Bank  of  Qinghai andRules  of 
Procedures  of  Shareholders’  Meeting  of  the  Bank  of  Qinghai,  the  Company  convoked  the  shareholders’  general 
meeting  for  year  2016.  The  convoking  procedures  of  the  conference  were  in  conformity  with  laws  and  regulations,
guaranteed  equal  status  of  shareholders,  in  particular  to  medium  and  small  sized  shareholders  and  ensured  the 
shareholders’ participating in the meeting and exercising voting rights.i1.3 About directors and the Board of Directors 
The 4th session of the Board of Directors of the Company is composed of 9 directors, including 2 independent 
directors.  All  the  directors  are  natural  persons,  the  directors’  qualiﬁcations  and  engagement  procedures  are  in 
conformity with the Articles of Association of the Bank of Qinghai, Election of Directors and Supervisors of the Bank of 
Qinghai  and  relevant  laws,  rules  and  regulations,  with  required  knowledge  and  quality  required  for  exercising  duties,
and the qualiﬁcations have been approved by Qinghai Bank Supervision Authorities.In the year 2017, the Company convoked 18 meetings of the Board of Directors, reviewed and voted 42 issues.
Decision  making,  authorization  and  voting  by  the  Board  of  Directors  shall  be  strictly  in  accordance  with  the  Articles 
of Association of the Bank of Qinghai, the Rules of Procedures of Meetings of the Board of Directors of the Bank of 
Qinghai and relevant rules and regulations. The Directors exercised duties, attended the meetings, reviewed key issues
related  to  the  Company’s  development,  issued  opinions  and  suggestions  independently,  and  were  dedicated  and
diligent to safeguard the Company, shareholders and other related parties’ lawful rights and interests.40(cid:952)(cid:19490)(cid:812)(cid:815)(cid:5024)(cid:5024)(cid:5074)(cid:6097)(cid:2422)VII. Information of the Company’s GoverningThe Board of Directors of the Company is composed of Strategic Development Commission, Risk Management 
and Related Transaction Control Commission, Remuneration and Assessment Commission, Nomination Commission 
and Audit Commission.1.4 About supervisors and the Board of Supervisors 
The  4th  Session  of  the  Board  of  Directors  of  the  Company  is  composed  of  7  supervisors,  and  the  job 
qualiﬁcations and engagement procedures are in accordance with the Articles of Association of the Bank of Qinghai, 
Election of Directors and Supervisors of the Bank of Qinghai and relevant laws and regulations. During the reporting
period,  the  Board  of  Supervisors  convoked  6  meetings,  reviewed  and  voted  11  issues.  All  the  supervisors  strictly
observed the Articles of Association of the Bank of Qinghai and the Rules of Procedures of the Board of Supervisors of 
the Bank of Qinghai, exercised duties, reinforced supervision, standardized operation, avoided risks, established and 
improved  scientiﬁc  and  effective  internal  supervision  mechanism,  fully  played  supervision  authorities  of  the  Board  of
Supervisors and safeguarded rights of the shareholders, public, the Company and staff.A Supervision Board is established under the Board of Supervisors of the Company.1.5 About information disclosure and investors relationship management 
During  the  reporting  period,  the  Company  strictly  observed  the Disclosure  Methods  of  Commercial  Bank 
Information and Disclosure Management of Commercial Bank Information and regulated disclosure of daily information. 
The  Company  disclosed  the  Company’s  annual  report,  key  information  and  the  shareholders’  meeting  information
timely,  accurately,  authentically  and  completely,  ensured  that  all  the  shareholders  had  equal  opportunities  to  obtain
information,  and  safeguarded  rights  and  interests  of  all  shareholders,  in  particular  to  medium  and  small-sized
shareholders. The Annual Report of the Bank of Qinghai for Year 2016 (Abstract) was published at the Financial Times
on  April  26,  2017  and  was  also  released  at  China  Money  Website  and  China  Bond  Website  to  accept  supervision 
by  the  public.  After  printing  of  offprint  of  the  Annual  Report  of  the  Bank  of  Qinghai  for  Year  2016,  it  was  posted  to 
the  government  authorities,  supervision  authorities,  main  shareholders  and  key  accounts  to  expand  the  scope  of 
information disclosure and reading and safeguard knowing rights of the shareholders and other interested parties.The  Company  establishes  a  special  department  to  receive  calls,  letters,  visiting  and  consultations  from 
shareholders,  contact  investors,  strengthens  the  investors’  knowing  and  trust  of  the  Company  and  establishes  a
faithful, stable and healthy and standard market image.2.  The Company’s operation and decision-making systemThe  Party  Committee  is  the  Company’s  political  core  and  leading  core,  is  responsible  for  researching  “three-
importance and one-large” issue, is the prepositive procedure for rules of procedures by the Board of Directors, the
Board  of  Supervisors  and  the  Operation  tier,  and  supports  the  Shareholders’  Assembly,  the  Board  of  Directors,  the
Board  of  Supervisors  and  senior  management  to  exercise  duties  according  to  laws;  the  Shareholders’  Assembly  is 
the Company’s top power organization of the Company and makes decisions, manages and supervises through the 
Board of Directors and the Board of Supervisors; the Board of Directors is the Company’s decision-making structure, 
is responsible for the Shareholders’ Assembly and is responsible for decisions by the Company’s key issues; the Board
of  Supervisors  is  the  internal  supervision  structure  of  the  Company,  is  responsible  to  the  Shareholders’  Assembly 
and  is  responsible  for  supervising  the  Board  of  Directors  and  the  senior  management;  the  Board  of  Supervisors  is
the  Company’s  internal  supervision  structure,  is  responsible  to  the  Shareholders’  Assembly  and  is  responsible  for 
supervising  the  Board  of  Directors  and  senior  management;  the  senior  management  is  the  Company’s  executingANNUAL REPORT 201741VII. Information of the Company’s Governingstructure,  is  responsible  to  the  Board  of  Directors,  carries  out  business  activities  according  to  authorization  by  the
Board of Directors and accepts supervision by the Board of Supervisors. The Company applies tier-1 juristic persons 
system, its branches are non-independent accounting organizations, and the management and business activities are
carried out according to the authorization by the head ofﬁce and the branches are responsible to the head ofﬁce.The Company has no controlling shareholders and actual controllers. The Company and major shareholders are 
independent in business, staff, assets, structures and ﬁnance. The Company is an independent juristic person running 
independently and suffering from losses on its own, and has independent and complete business and self-operation 
capabilities.3.  The Company’s branchesThe Company has 82 business networks, including 6 branches, 5 administration banks, 3 directly afﬁliated sub-branches, 62 tier-2 sub-branches and 5 community branches and 1 small-sized ﬁnancial service center.4. business  was  stable  and  healthy. Firstly,  the Management  on  Overall  Risks  of  the  Bank  of  Qinghai was
drafted to establish an overall risk management system to ensure that the risk management were complete. 
Secondly,  the  Board  of  Directors  reinforced  risk  management  building,  supplemented  the  risk  prevention 
and  control  system  and  ensured  that  each  business  and  each  product  should  be  observed. Thirdly,  the
Board of Directors managed the existing credit risks and increment credit risk monitoring, alert, control and
dissolving,  expanding  handling  channels  and  improved  achievements.  In  particular,  the  Board  of  Directors 
should  manage  disposal  of  the  non-conforming  loans  to  achieve  fruitful  results.  Meanwhile,  the  Board  of
Directors  managed  existing  credit  risks,  alert,  control  and  dissolving,  expanded  disposal  channels  and
improved handling effects. In particular, the Board of Directors closely concerned, managed and dissolved
market risks, operation risks, reputation risks, the employees’ morality risks etc. to ensure that there were
no cases or accidents during the year. Fourthly, according to the supervision requirements and taking the
Company’s situations into the Company, the Board of Directors managed provision in particular to provision
and accrual of non-credit loan assets and managed risk buffering. Fifthly, the Board of Directors reinforced
the conformance culture building, reinforced the staff’s morality and occupational behavior education, and

University  to  establish  “Bank  of  Qinghai  Postgraduate  Workstation”  and  “College  Postgraduate  Innovation
and  Practice  Base”  to  reinforce  college-enterprise  cooperation  and  reﬁne  ﬁnancial  research  and  strategic
management of the Bank of Qinghai.ANNUAL REPORT 201757X. Report by the Board of Supervisors1.  Work by the Board of Directors for Year 2017(1)Fully  implemented  the  special  inspection  of  “two  reinforcements  and  two  inhibitions”  and  review”  and 
reinforced  supervision  over  risk  management  and  control.  According  to  requirements  in  the  Notice  on
Correction  and  Accountability  of  “Two  Reinforcements  and  Two  Inhibitions”  by  the  Ofﬁce  of  the  China 
Banking  Regulatory  Commission,  based  on  the  pre-stage  Implementation  Proposal  for  Correction  and 
Accountability of “Two Reinforcement and Two Inhibitions” by the Bank of Qinghai, the breaching operation
of the banking industry was taken into annual key works of the Board of Supervisors and was deployed with
“three breaching”, “three arbitrages” and “four improperness”. The Board of Directors reinforced importance 
of  the  accountability,  supervised  the  correction  work  in  stages,  required  the  internal  audit  departments  to 
assign the duties to speciﬁc departments and personnel and ensure orderly operation of the correction. In 
the  process  of  correction,  requirements  were  clariﬁed,  the  correction  time  limit,  correction  measures  and 
correction  objectives  were  implemented,  dynamic  work,  testing  and  supervision  were  reinforced.  As  for 
issued to be corrected immediately; if the correction is temporarily difﬁcult, detailed and feasible correction 
plans were drafted and any breaching operation and safety hidden troubles of breaching shall be invested 
and punished and one case shall be punished if discovered.(2) Reinforcing  inspection  of  ﬁnancial  management.  The  Board  of  Supervisor  shall  closely  focus  on  and
supervise  execution  of  indexes  affecting  ﬁnancial  beneﬁts  and  supervise  execution  of  budget  approved
by  the  Board  of  Directors;  supervise  execution  of  ﬁnancial  revenue  and  expenditures  of  the  branches  and 
use  and  management  of  the  allocated  expenses;  supervise  and  check  authenticity  of  ﬁnancial  accounting 
and  annual  proﬁts;  and  perform  special  supervision  and  inspection  over  key  expenditures  and  propose
suggestions and opinions on ﬁnancial management.(3) Reinforcing  investigation  over  performance  of  directors  and  senior  management.  Through  attending  the 
meetings  of  the  Board  of  Directors  as  non-voting  delegates  and  periodically  participating  in  business
analysis  conference,  the  Board  of  Directors  supervises  the  directors’  performance  in  decision-making  and 
risk  management  control,  supervises  the  senior  management’s  enforcement  in  decision-making  by  the 
Board  of  Directors,  supervises  performance  of  the  senior  management  in  driving  business  transformation
and lean management enforcement and sensitivity and handling of risk management and control. The Board
of  Supervisors  improves  the  assessment  and  reporting  system,  investigates  and  supervises  performance
by  the  Board  of  Directors  and  senior  management  in  various  views  and  plays  the  roles  of  “observer”  and
“supervisor” by the Board of Supervisors.(4)Improving the supervision mechanism and supervision quality. In year 2017, the Board of Supervisors and the 
Board of Directors organized and guided the internal audit department to expand overage of audit for business
activities, which were increased in terms of varieties, scopes and quantities of the audit. Compared with the 
last  years,  the  scope  of  audit  was  not  only  limited  to  fundamental  business  such  as  “ﬁnance”,  “accounting” 
or “credit loan”, with combination of “regular audit”, “special audit” to cover all ﬁelds of business, monitor and 
discover weak procedures in business, implement internal control and effectively control business risks of the
Bank. In the process of audit, the key points of audit were transferred to previous data veriﬁcation to internal 
control  and  management;  in  the  feedback  of  regular  audit  issues,  importance  and  necessity  of  the  internal
control system are highlighted and feasible corrective suggestions were proposed.Meanwhile,  to  improve  internal  management  and  control  of  the  Bank,  promote  conformance  business, 
guarantee safety, stable and healthy operation of business and ensure orderly operation of internal control
and  assessment,  the  Board  of  Supervisors  consigns  the  Audit  Department  to  carry  out  internal  control 
assessment  on  branches  and  departments  of  the  head  ofﬁce  for  year  2016. and  inspection  achievements  made  by  the  internal  audit  department,  dispatched  Board  of  Supervisors
of  the  State-owned  Committee  and  the  Banking  Regulatory  Commission  were  fully  yielded  to  advance 
tracking and correction. Communication and coordination with the Board of Directors of the Company, the
Business Management and the supervision authorities shall be fully supported and coordinated to promote 
sustainable  and  healthy  development  of  Company.  During  the  reporting  period,  the  Board  of  Supervisors
convoked 6 meetings of the Board of Supervisors in ﬁeld and telecommunication and reviewed 11 proposals
such as annual report, ﬁnancial budget and ﬁnal settlement plans, proﬁt distribution plans and work report 
by the Board of Supervisors. During the period, the supervisors performed duties carefully, reviewed each 
key topic and fully released opinions and suggestions.2.Independent opinions on relevant issues by the Board of Supervisors 
During  the  reporting  period,  according  to  the  Guide  to  Governing  of  Commercial  Bank  Company,  Work  Guide
to Board of Supervisors of Commercial Bank and relevant laws, rules and regulations and the 
Articles of Association 
of the Bank of Qinghai, through attending meetings of the Board of Directors and meetings of senior management as 
non-voting delegates, daily operation supervision, non-ﬁeld monitoring, reviewing report and face-to-face interview, the
Board of Supervisors exercised supervision duties for directors, supervisors and senior managers, taking performance
requirements  on  directors,  supervisors  and  senior  management  of  the  stock  commercial  banks,  and  the  Board  of 
Supervisors  assess  performance  of  the  directors,  supervisors  and  senior  management  for  year  2017  objectives  and 
fairly, with assessment opinions as follows:k(1) Assessment opinions on performance of the Board of Directors and the members  
The Board of Supervisors holds the opinions that, ﬁrstly, the Board of Directors fully played the decision-making
function. In year 2017, the Board of Directors judged the macroscopic economic situations, actively tackled the new
supervision rules, considered the Company’s actual situations and encountered difﬁculties, explored new development
philosophy,  managed  the  development  trend  and  drafted  new  development  strategy.  According  to  authorization  by
the  Shareholders’  General  Meeting,  the  Company  made  scientiﬁc  decision-making  in  terms  of  corporate  governing, 
risk  control,  senior  management  engagement  and  innovative  transformation  etc.,  timely  issued  the  Guide  Opinions 
on  Further  Reinforcement  of  Capital  Management,  Guide  Opinions  on  Implementation  of  Relevant  Supervision
Requirements  and  other  guide  documents  within  the  year  and  undertook  the  ﬁnal  objectives  for  the  Company’s 
business  and  management. Secondly,  the  Board  of  Directors  continues  to  reinforce  strategy  control  and  advance 
new  progress.  The  4th  increase  in  capital  and  share  which  has  been  prepared  for  many  years  achieved  substantial
progress,  and  the  pre-stage  preparation  was  almost  ﬁnished.  The  procedures  for  applying  for  consumption  ﬁnancial 
company  has  been  accelerated.  The  corporate  governing  system  was  improved,  the  Party  building  was  written  into
the Articles of Association, the Party building of the state-owned enterprise and the corporate juristic person governing
structure  were  united  and  the  new  corporate  governing  mode  of  “Shareholders’  Assembly,  Board  of  Supervisors,
Board  of  Directors,  Operation  Tier  and  Senior  Management”  has  been  formed.  The Rules  and  Regulations  on
Authorities  of  Basic  Authorization  of  the  Bank  of  Qinghai  was  revised  to  clarify  responsibilities  and  duties  boundary 
of  the  Board  of  Directors  and  senior  management.  The  risk  management  and  control  are  fruitful  and  are  controlled 
acceptable  to  the  Company. Thirdly,  all  the  directors  demonstrated  strong  sense  of  responsibility  and  high-quality
character, actively participated in discussion, made independent, professional and objective judgment for development 
strategy,  business  plan  and  risk  prevention  and  control,  their  own  opinions  and  suggestions  were  released  and  the 
work of the Board of Directors was carried out as usual. The independent director released objective and fair opinionsANNUAL REPORT 201759X. Report by the Board of Supervisorsfor issues discussed by the Board of Directors. The Executive Director reported the Company’s business and relevant 
information  to  the  Board  of  Directors  completely,  authentically  and  timely,  guaranteed  that  the  Board  of  Directors
and  the  members  could  fully  know  about  the  Company’s  operation  and  managed  assessment  on  the  Company  by
the  supervision  authorities,  external  audit  organization  and  social  public.  The  Non-executive  Director  concerned 
implementation  of  resolutions  of  the  Board  of  Directors  by  the  senior  management  on  a  long-term  basis,  managed 
communication  between  the  Company  and  shareholders  and  avoided  any  behaviors  that  shareholders’  rights  and 
interests above the Company and other shareholders. Fourthly, through daily supervision, the commissions under the
Board of Director were lack of independence and some directors failed to participate in the meeting of the Board of 
Directors and their performance was insufﬁcient.(2) Opinions on performance assessment on senior management and members 
The  Board  of  Supervisors  holds  the  opinions  that, ﬁrstly, based  on  business  and  development  objectives 
determined  the  Party  Committee  and  the  Board  of  Directors  of  the  Bank,  senior  management  of  the  Company 
strictly  executes  resolutions  adopted  by  the  Board  of  Directors  and  the  Board  of  Supervisors  and  carried  out
operation  and  management  activities  in  accordance  with  the  Articles  of  Association  of  the  Bank  of  Qinghai  and
authorization  by  the  Board  of  Directors.  The  senior  management  adheres  to  the  principle  of  ﬁnancial  service  entity 
serving  economic  entity,  develops  inclusive  ﬁnance,  green  ﬁnance,  livelihood  ﬁnance  and  science  and  technology 
ﬁnance  and  continues  to  increase  investment  on  investment;  reinforces  brand  awareness,  carries  forward  “brand 
ﬁrst”  strategy  and  forms  the  ﬁnancial  service  brand  system  with  features  of  the  Company.  Secondly,  the  Company
moves forwards of transformation of lean management structure, development route, business structure, organization
structure  and  management  mode  and  strengthens  intrinsic  power  of  business  and  development.  Thirdly,  the  senior
management  adheres  to  simultaneous  arrangement  and  deployment  of  risk  prevention  and  control  and  operation,
continues  to  improve  risk  prevention  and  control  and  dissolving  capability,  and  all  the  staff  raises  the  awareness  of 
observing  disciplines  and  code  and  controls  risks  effectively. Fourthly,  the  senior  management  develops  corporate
culture building, deepens innovation culture, management culture and ten cultures in total in the mind, and promote
and  combine  with  operation  and  development.  The  senior  management  actively  exercises  social  responsibilities 
of  local  juristic  persons  and  enhances  corporate  image.  Fifthly,  facing  severe  economic  ﬁnancial  situations  and 
development  difﬁculties,  the  senior  management  makes  efforts,  challenges  difﬁculties,  actively  yields  the  subjective 
initiative, explores new development route and contributes to transformation and development. Meanwhile, the senior
management  plays  the  role  of  leading,  unite  and  leads  the  upper  and  lower  tiers  to  embody  work,  implement  job 
responsibilities, drive the Company’s business to achieve new breakthroughs and obtain new achievements. Sixthly,
through daily supervision and ﬁndings, the senior management of the Company further reinforces internal management
and control, system building and risk prompts etc.i(3) Assessment opinions on performance of the Board of Supervisors and members 
The Board of Supervisors holds the opinions that, ﬁrstly, all the supervisors shall participate in the meeting of Board 
of  Supervisors  and  supervise  meetings  of  the  Board  of  Supervisors  according  to  laws  and  the Articles  of  Association
of  the  Bank  of  Qinghai  and  release  opinions  and  suggestions  for  the  issues. 
Secondly,  the  Executive  Supervisors 
attend  meetings  of  the  Board  of  Directors  and  meetings  of  the  senior  management  when  appropriate  based  on  work 
needs, timely know about development and management of the Company, exercise performance duties and effectively 
safeguard lawful rights and interest of the Company, shareholders, staff, creditors and other interested persons. Thirdly,
in  terms  of  “performance  by  the  Board  of  Supervisors  not  in  placement”  by  Qinghai  Banking  Regulatory  Commission 
at  the  site  of  “Board  of  Directors,  Board  of  Supervisors  and  Operation  Tier”,  the  Board  of  Supervisors  corrects  and 
overcomes the shortcomings, further clariﬁes key assessment points on performance of directors, supervisors and senior 
management by the Board of Supervisors and key supervision and inspection points of operation and decision-making, 
risk  management  and  internal  control  by  the  Board  of  Directors,  reinforces  effective  supervision  over  the  remuneration

Report by the Board of Supervisors3.  Key points of the Board of Supervisors for year 2018(1) Reinforcing  supervision  over  risk  management  and  control.  The  Board  of  Supervisors  closely  focuses
and supervises risk control related to development of the Company, concerns key issues, key procedures
and possible issues and risk sources, supervises policies, procedures and measures implementation by the
Board of Directors and Operation Tier in key issues. The Board of Supervisors supervises application of risk 
prevention measures during operation, further reinforces supervision over case prevention and control and
promotes safe and stable, stable and healthy development of the Bank. The Board of Supervisors reinforces 
supervision  over  ﬁnancial  management,  in  particular  to  ﬁnancial  budget  execution  approved  by  the  Board
of Director, execution of revenue and expenditures, management of allocated expenses and authenticity of
annual proﬁts, and reinforced supervision and inspection of key expenditure.(2) Reinforcing  application  of  supervision  achievements  by  the  Board  of  Supervisors.  The  Company
closely  focuses  on  implementation  of  the  supervision  requirements  by  the  Board  of  Directors  and  the 
Operation Tier and requires correction of the exposed issues by issuing the suggestion letters and reminding
letter  etc.  The  communication  and  coordination  mechanism  with  the  Board  of  Supervisors  dispatched  by 
the State-owned Assets Committee shall be improved to ensure that the Board of Supervisors achieves new
breakthroughs.(3) Reinforcing  assessment  and  supervision  and  assessment  over  directors,  supervisors  and  senior
management. We improve assessment and reporting systems for performance of directors, supervisors and
senior management, observe, supervise and assess performance in various views, and propose supervision
and  assessment  opinions  and  improvement  suggestions.  We  reinforce  communication  with  directors  and 
senior management, fully support work by the Board of Directors and the operation tier, provide suggestions
for work of the Bank, and raise the Company’s management to a new level.(4) Continuing to reinforce building of the Board of Supervisors. We reinforce the system training strength,
reinforce  theoretical  learning  and  business  training  of  members  of  the  Board  of  Supervisors,  improve
proﬁciency  of  the  supervisors  and  improve  the  supervisors’  performance.  We  work  in  terms  of  system,
training  mechanism,  self-discipline  and  information  building,  manage  the  performance  and  improve  the
company’s  governing  and  proﬁciency.  Combined  with  the  supervision  authorities’  new  requirements  on 
the  Company’s  governing  structure,  the  Company  further  improves  organizing  structure  of  the  Board
of  Supervisors.  With  opportunities  of  the  meeting  of  the  Board  of  Supervisors,  the  meeting  of  special
commissions,  attending  the  meeting  of  the  Board  of  Directors  and  analysis  conference  of  the  senior
management,  we  adopt  periodic  industrial  report,  special  business  communication,  in-ﬁeld  investigation 
and  research  and  other  methods  to  reinforce  the  supervisors’  analyzing  capabilities,  operation  capabilities
and their characters and improve performance of the Board of Supervisors. Based on effectively organizing
audit inspection, attending conference, daily observation and other supervision means, the Company further
innovates  in  supervision  and  management,  explores  to  establish  and  implement  the  tour  inspection  and
inquiry  mechanism  for  the  Board  of  Supervisors  and  carry  out  audit.  The  Board  of  Supervisors  performs 
special  and  comprehensive  investigation  and  research  activities  and  necessary  inquiries.  The  Company
closely  focuses  on  progress  of  control  of  breaching  activities  within  the  banking  industry,  reinforces

14,063,898,523.942ANNUAL REPORT 201777XII. Financial ReportThe  ﬁnancial  report  of  the  Company  for  year  2017  was  audited  by  Certiﬁed  Public  Accountant  of  Pan-China
Certiﬁed  Public  Account  (special  general  partnership)  Li  Bin  and  Wang  Junyao  in  accordance  with  the  independent 
audit code of the Certiﬁed Public Accountant, and the audit report and the audited ﬁnancial accounting statements are 
detailed as follows:Audit ReportT.J.S. [2018] No.8-88All shareholders of Bank of Qinghai Co., Ltd.,I.  Audit opinionsWe audited ﬁnancial statement of Bank of Qinghai Co., Ltd. (hereinafter referred to as Bank of Qinghai), including
consolidated and parent company’s balance sheet dated on December 31, 2007, consolidated and parent company’s 
proﬁt  statement,  consolidated  and  parent  company’s  cash  ﬂow  statement  and  consolidated  and  parent  company’s 
statement of change of owner’s equities for year 2017 and annotation to the ﬁnancial statements.We think that, the attached ﬁnancial statements are prepared in accordance with the corporate accounting code
in  key  aspects  to  reﬂect  ﬁnancial  situations  of  the  consolidated  and  the  parent  company  of  the  Bank  of  Qinghai  on
December 31, 2017 and the consolidated and parent company’s business achievements and cash ﬂow for year 2017.II.  Basis for audit opinionsWe  audited  according  to  rules  and  regulations  of  the  audit  code  of  the  Certiﬁed  Public  Account.  The 
“responsibilities  of  CPA  for  the  ﬁnancial  audit  report”  describes  our  responsibilities  under  these  codes.  According  to 
the occupational morality code of Certiﬁed Public Account of China, we are independent of the Bank of Qinghai and 
performed other responsibilities of occupational morality. We believe that, the audit evidences obtained are evident and 
proper to provide basis for issuing audit opinions.III.  The  Management’s  and  Government  Tier’s  responsibilities  for  the  ﬁnancialstatements 
The  Management  of  the  Bank  of  Qinghai  (hereinafter  referred  to  as  the  management)  prepared  the  ﬁnancial
statements in accordance with the corporate accounting code to make them fairly reﬂected, and designing, executing
and  maintaining  necessary  control  to  make  them  reﬂected  fairly,  and  designing,  executing  and  maintain  necessary 
internal control to make the ﬁnancial statements free of any misstatements by embezzlement or errors.When preparing the ﬁnancial statements, the management is responsible for assessing continuing capabilities of
the  Bank  of  Qinghai,  disclosing  issued  related  to  continuing  business  (if  applicable)  and  applying  the  assumption  of 
continuing business, unless liquidation, termination of operation or other inevitable choices.The  Governing  Tier  (hereinafter  referred  to  as  the  Governing  Tier)  of  the  Bank  of  Qinghai  is  responsible  forsupervising ﬁnancial reporting process of the Bank of Qinghai.IV.  CPA’s responsibilities for audit of ﬁnancial statementsOur objective is to obtain reasonable guarantees for the ﬁnancial statements without embezzlement or errors and
issue audit report with audit opinions. The reasonable guarantee is a high-level guarantee but cannot guarantee a key
error could be always found on the date of audit. The misstatement may be caused by embezzlement or errors. If the
reasonable errors summed up or collected may affect use of the ﬁnancial statement or any decisions made, the error is
signiﬁcant.78(cid:952)(cid:19490)(cid:812)(cid:815)(cid:5024)(cid:5024)(cid:5074)(cid:6097)(cid:2422)XII. Financial ReportIn the process of audit, we apply occupational judgment and keep occupational suspect. Meanwhile, we executethe following work:(I)Identifying  and  assessing  key  error  risks  by  embezzlement  or  errors,  designing  and  implementing  audit
procedures to tackle these risks and obtain sufﬁcient and proper audit evidences as the basis for releasing
opinions. For the embezzlement may involve collusion, falsiﬁcation, deliberated omission and false statement
or is above internal control, the risks of key errors by the embezzlement higher than the risks by errors are 
not found.(II)  Knowing about internal control related to audit to design proper audit procedures, not to issue opinions oneffectiveness of internal control.(III) Assessing properness of accounting policy and rationality of accounting estimate and relevant disclosures.(IV)  Providing  conclusion  on  properness  of  continuing  business  assumptions.  Meanwhile,  according  to 
evidences  obtained,  the  conclusion  of  issues  or  situations  on  continuing  business  by  the  Bank  of  Qinghai 
was  obtained.  If  the  conclusion  shows  uncertainty,  the  audit  code  requires  us  to  require  the  report  users 
to notice disclosures in the ﬁnancial statements; if the disclosure is insufﬁcient, we require the report users
to  notice  the  disclosures  in  the  ﬁnancial  reports;  if  the  disclosure  is  insufﬁcient,  we  shall  release  reserve
opinions. Our conclusion is based on information obtained from the date of the audit report. However, the 
future events may result in the Bank of Qinghai failure to operate.(V)  Assessing  general  statement,  structure  and  content  (including  disclosure)  of  the  ﬁnancial  statements,  andassessing whether the ﬁnancial statements reﬂect relevant transactions and issued.(VI)  Obtaining  sufﬁcient  and  proper  audit  evidences  for  ﬁnancial  information  in  physical  or  business  activities
and  releasing  audit  opinions  for  the  ﬁnancial  statements.  We  are  responsible  for  guiding,  supervising  and
executing the group design and bear all responsibilities for the audit.We  communicated  with  the  governing  tier  in  respect  of  the  scope  of  audit,  schedule  and  key  audit  ﬁndings,including internal control defects identiﬁed in the audit.Pan-China Certiﬁed Public Account-ChChChinininnnaa aaa Ceeertrtrtrtr iﬁeddd PP Pubbbbblililill ccc cc Accccc
